		icon = GFX_decision_oppression_rev
		
		visible = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = radical_socialism 
				has_government = communism
			}
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = POL_seim_commun
				has_country_flag = POL_seim_radsoc
				has_country_flag = POL_seim_socdem
				has_country_flag = POL_seim_mrklib

				has_country_flag = POL_seim_author
				has_country_flag = POL_seim_antogonism
				has_country_flag = POL_seim_soclib
			}
		}
		available = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = radical_socialism
				has_government = communism
			}
			OR = {
				any_country = { has_war_with = ROOT has_government = communism }
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = "Антагонизм сейма более 60%"
					check_variable = { POL_seim_antogonism > 0.60 }
				}
			}
			communism > 0.15
		}
		cost = 15
		days_remove = 7
		fire_only_once = yes
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 999
		}
		
		remove_effect = {
			add_stability = -0.1
			custom_effect_tooltip = POL_zapret_commun_tt
			set_country_flag = POL_zapret_commun
			add_popularity = { ideology = communism popularity = -0.05 }
		}
	}

	#Миссии рад-соцев
	
	POL_radsoc_mission_miting = {
		icon = GFX_decision_radsoc_organize_strike_two
		activation = {
			always = no
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = POL_seim_commun
				has_country_flag = POL_seim_socdem
				has_country_flag = POL_seim_soclib
				has_country_flag = POL_seim_mrklib
				has_country_flag = POL_seim_conser
				has_country_flag = POL_seim_despot
				has_country_flag = POL_seim_author
				has_country_flag = POL_seim_antogonism
			}
		}
		available = {
			has_government = radical_socialism
		}
		visible = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = POL_seim_radsoc }
		}
		fire_only_once = yes
		is_good = yes
		days_mission_timeout = 28
		timeout_effect = {
			add_popularity = { ideology = radical_socialism popularity = 0.01 }
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = POL_seim_radsoc_yacheiki } }
					activate_mission = POL_radsoc_mission_yacheiki
					remove_mission = POL_radsoc_mission_miting
				}
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { POL_seim_antogonism > 0.30 } radical_socialism > 0.15 }
					activate_mission = POL_radsoc_mission_krestyan_myatesh
					remove_mission = POL_radsoc_mission_miting
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = POL_seim_radsoc_yacheiki }
					activate_mission = POL_radsoc_mission_debation_seim
					remove_mission = POL_radsoc_mission_miting
				}
			}
		}
	}

	POL_socdem_mission_miting_rab = {
		icon = GFX_decision_socdem_political_discourse
		activation = {
			always = no
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = POL_seim_commun
				has_country_flag = POL_seim_radsoc
				has_country_flag = POL_seim_soclib
				has_country_flag = POL_seim_mrklib
				has_country_flag = POL_seim_conser
				has_country_flag = POL_seim_despot
				has_country_flag = POL_seim_author
				has_country_flag = POL_seim_antogonism
			}
		}
		available = {
			has_government = social_democracy
		}
		visible = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = POL_seim_socdem }
		}
		fire_only_once = yes
		is_good = yes
		days_mission_timeout = 28
		timeout_effect = {
			add_popularity = { ideology = social_democracy popularity = 0.01 }
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = POL_socdem_mission } }
					activate_mission = POL_socdem_mission_kritic_trud
					remove_mission = POL_socdem_mission_miting_rab
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = POL_socdem_mission }
					activate_mission = POL_socdem_mission_protiv_rev
					remove_mission = POL_socdem_mission_miting_rab
				}
				if = {
					limit = { 
						social_democracy > 0.3 
						social_democracy > party_popularity@communism
						social_democracy > party_popularity@radical_socialism
						social_democracy > party_popularity@market_liberalism
						social_democracy > party_popularity@social_liberalism
						social_democracy > party_popularity@despotism
						social_democracy > party_popularity@authoritarism
						social_democracy > party_popularity@conservatism
						social_democracy > party_popularity@fascism
						social_democracy > party_popularity@national_syndicalism
					}
					activate_mission = POL_socdem_mission_create_kabinet_pps
					remove_mission = POL_socdem_mission_miting_rab
				}
			}
		}
	}

				if = {

					}

				remove_mission = POL_soclib_mission_protest_land

					}

					remove_mission = POL_soclib_mission_protest_land
				}
			}
		}

		}

			add_popularity = { ideology = social_democracy popularity = -0.01 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = social_liberalism popularity = -0.01 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = conservatism popularity = 0.01 }
			POL_inf_p_bar = yes
			POL_reset_seim_antogonism = yes
			POL_antogonism_seim_rise_02 = yes
			POL_seim_reset_effect_idea = yes
			hidden_effect = {
				activate_mission = POL_conser_mission_debation_seim
				remove_mission = POL_conser_mission_protiv_left
				if = {
					limit = { 
						conservatism > 0.3 
						conservatism > party_popularity@communism
						conservatism > party_popularity@radical_socialism
						conservatism > party_popularity@market_liberalism
						conservatism > party_popularity@social_democracy
						conservatism > party_popularity@despotism
						conservatism > party_popularity@authoritarism
						conservatism > party_popularity@social_liberalism
						conservatism > party_popularity@fascism
						conservatism > party_popularity@national_syndicalism
					}
					activate_mission = POL_conser_mission_create_kabinet_pps
					remove_mission = POL_conser_mission_protiv_left
				}
			}
		}
	}

	POL_despot_mission_propogand_kult = {
		icon = GFX_decision_despot_pilsudski
		activation = {
			always = no
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = POL_seim_commun
				has_country_flag = POL_seim_radsoc
				has_country_flag = POL_seim_socdem
				has_country_flag = POL_seim_mrklib
				has_country_flag = POL_seim_soclib
				has_country_flag = POL_seim_conser
				has_country_flag = POL_seim_author
				has_country_flag = POL_seim_antogonism
			}
		}
		available = {
			has_government = despotism has_country_flag = POL_seim_despot
		}
		visible = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = POL_seim_despot }
		}
		fire_only_once = yes
		is_good = yes
		days_mission_timeout = 28
		timeout_effect = {
			add_popularity = { ideology = despotism popularity = 0.01 }
			hidden_effect = {
				activate_mission = POL_despot_mission_sobranie_legion
				remove_mission = POL_despot_mission_propogand_kult
				IF = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							AND = {
								has_country_leader = { name = "Józef Pilsudski" ruling_only = yes }								
								custom_trigger_tooltip = {
									tooltip = "Влияние начальника абсолютное или выше"
									check_variable = { var = POL_seim_vlinyanie value = 8 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
								}
								check_variable = { POL_seim_antogonism > 0.50 }
							}
							AND = {
								has_country_leader = { name = "Józef Pilsudski" ruling_only = yes }								
								custom_trigger_tooltip = {
									tooltip = "Влияние начальника абсолютное или выше"
									check_variable = { var = POL_seim_vlinyanie value = 8 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
								}
								has_stability < 0.25
								check_variable = { POL_seim_antogonism > 0.30 }
							}
							AND = {
								despotism > 0.2
								check_variable = { POL_seim_antogonism > 0.80 }
							}
							AND = {
								despotism > 0.1
								check_variable = { POL_seim_antogonism > 0.50 }
								 has_stability < 0.15
							}
						}
					}
					activate_mission = POL_despot_mission_reshim_sanation
					remove_mission = POL_despot_mission_propogand_kult
				}
			}
		}
	}

		}
